## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
  [*] --> Idle
  Idle --> FileSelected : select file -> setImportFile
  FileSelected --> ReadyToUpload : file present
  ReadyToUpload --> Uploading : click Upload -> read file
  Uploading --> Success : response.status == 200
  Uploading --> Failure : response.isLoadingError
  Success --> [*]
  Failure --> [*]
```
